 yah vidheyak us ardinance kii jagah aayaa he jo is saal janvari main laayaa gaya tha
 Efforts were on since 2010 to make the Medical Council of India clean and transparent
 janvari main laayaa gaya ardinance isi kii agali kadi thi
 The government twice tried to replace the MCI with a new regulatory body
 pehali baar 2011 main neshnal council of human resorcej in health (NCHRH) ke rup main or duusari baar 2017 main neshnal medical kamishan (NMC) ke rup main
 But both these attempts failed
 kendriya swasthya mantri harshavardhan ne kaha ki emsiai apane kaam ko sahi tareeke se puraa karne main vifal or bhrashtachar main lipt rahi he
 MCI was first taken under control in 2010 when its chairman Ketan Desai was arrested by the CBI
 un par punjab ke ek medical college ko manyata dene ke liye 2 karod rupee rishwat lene kaa aarope laga tha
 In 2016, a parliamentary panel investigated the working of the MCI and found that it had a long list of complaints against it
 jaanch main javabdehi or paardarshita kii kami, anivaary jimmedaariyon ko puraa nahin kar paanaa, bhrashtachar, snaatak or parasnatak shiksha main kharaab niyaman or kamjor niyantran jaisi kamiyaan ujgar huikya kahata he vidheyakayah vidheyak do saal ke liye chuni jane vaali emsiai ko nishprabhavi karte hue isaki shaktiyaan sarkaar kii ore se niyukt board aaf governors ko detaa he
 The board would have 12 members, while MCI consisted of 7 members
 vidheyak main sadasyon kii yogyata ko lekar bhi nae praavdhaan kiye gaye hai
 Now the Board of Governors will also include experts with 'administrative ability and experience' in addition to medical doctors
 board kii sahaayta ke liye ek secretary general hoga jise centre sarkaar niyukt karegi
 He will be the head of the council's secretariat
 bill paas hone tak lanbaa sangharshemasiai ko javabdeh banane kii prakriya 2009 main shuru ho gai thi
 When the President announced the establishment of the National Council of Human Resources in Health (NCHRH), a regulatory body for the entire medical field
 yah kushal peshewaron kii aapurti ke liye niamak sanstha main sudhaar kii ek pahal thi
 Under this, a separate council was to be formed for higher education and health
 2010 main is prakriya ne raftaar pakad lee jab emsiai ke adhyaksh ko giraftaar kiya gaya or sarkaar ne iske sanchaalan ko apane niyantran main lete hue ek ardinance ke jariye saat sadasyeey board aaf governors kii niyukti kar di
 Initially this system was for one year but later it was extended till 2013
 isi bich 2011 main ek nai niamak sanstha kii sthapana ke liye NCHRH bill pesh kiya gaya lekin ek sansadeey panel ne suzav diya ki ise waapas le liya janaa chahie or paryaapt raishumaari or shankaaon ke samaadhaan ke saath ise phir se draft kiya janaa chahie
 However, in 2013 the government failed to reinstate MCI through adequate legal process and MCI remained in its old form till 2018
 is dauraan sanstha ke khilaaf nae bhrashtachar ke maamle saamne aae, jo supreme court main pahunch gaya or isaki nigaraanee ke liye do baar nirikshan samitiyaan baniin
 In 2018, the second oversight committee resigned saying that MCI did not follow its instructions
 iske chalate 2018 main phir se sarkaar ne ek ardinance ke jariye ise apane niyantran main le liya
 As an alternative to the MCI, the government introduced the National Medical Commission (NMC) Bill 2017 in the Lok Sabha but due to several reasons, this bill was also clouded
 isamen se pratinidhitiv nadaarad tha
 As such, elected medical professionals and state representatives were not given place
 privet medical college main fees kii vyavastha main samasya thi or saath hi yah bhi sifarish thi ki doctoron ko aayush-ayurveda, yoga, unani, homeopathy aadi ke 'brij course' karaaen jaaen or doctors unhen bhi apane sujhaavon main shaamil karen
 The parliamentary panel oversaw the NMC Bill and suggested several changes to it
 panel ne vidheyak main pratinidhitiv badhaane ke saath yah bhi suzav diya ki aayush ke 'brij course' ko anivaary na kiya jaae
 This was later accepted by the government
 haalanki, NMC vidheyak dobaaraa nahin laayaa gaya or pichhali loksabhaa main swat: hi radd ho gaya
 Why oppose the bill? The Indian Medical Association (IMA), a representative body of doctors in India, has strongly opposed taking MCI under government control
 IMA ke purv adhyaksh dow
 KK Aggarwal says that it is not in the interest of society and democracy to take away the autonomy of any regulatory body
 unhone kaha, “jaise aap sansad ko sirf cabinet ke nirnyon se nahin chalaa sakate yaa bina donon sadanon se paas kiye bagaiyr nahin chalaa sakate, thik usee tarah emsiai ko chalaane ke liye aapako ek akjicutive body or council chahie
 On the allegations of corruption on MCI, he says that the government can remedy it if it wants to, without taking away its autonomy and taking appropriate action
 IMA ke ek or purv adhyaksh dow
 Vinay Aggarwal also expresses similar views
 unhone NMC kaa bhi virodh kiya tha
 They state that such institutions must be essentially democratic, representative, and autonomous
 kisi niamak sanstha ko majboot karne ke liye 10 saal kaa samay kisi bhi sarkaar ke liye bahut hota he
 The government should be cautious and careful
 jaisaa ki pichley 10 saal se hota rahaa, ardinance or ek vidheyak ke badale duusare vidheyak laane kii jagah sarkaar ko salaah or yojana ke jariye dirghakaalik samaadhaan khojna chahie

 ' Team India's batsmen are considered the best in terms of spin, but in the Test series released in England, Moin Ali has so far kept the Indian batsmen on their spin
 4 test maichon main moin ke khate main 19 wicket ja chuke hai or bhartiya ballebaaj unki phiraki ko pard paane main laachaar se najar aa rahe hai
 But former cricketer and former India spinner Bishan Singh Bedi believes that Moin is an ordinary spinner
 bedi ne kaha ki moin na hi koi mistry bowler hai or na hi top class spinner
 Due to the helplessness of Indian batsmen in front of Moin, this spinner has become the fastest spinner to take 20 wickets in Test cricket from England
 bhartiya ballebaajon ko spin gendbaaji khilne ke liye janaa jaataa he, lekin maujuuda siries main 27 saal ke moin ne puri team india kii naak main dam kar rakhaa he
 Batsmen like Virat Kohli and Cheteshwar Pujara have also been out on this spinner's ball
 bedi ne kaha, 'kisi ko bhartiya ballebaajon se poochna chahie ki wo is spinner ko kaise rate karenge? jahaan tak meraa sawaal he, mere hisaab se wo old-faishand of-brake bowler he, isse zyada kuch nahin

 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) The All India Muslim Personal Law Board has filed its affidavit in the Supreme Court on petitions challenging the provision to end the marriage by saying divorce thrice
 board ne maang kii he ki tripal talaak ko chunauti dene vaali yachikaaon ko khaarij kiya janaa chahie
 Significantly, in another case, a two-judge bench of the Supreme Court took cognizance of itself and requested Chief Justice TS Thakur to set up a special bench and look into the case of Muslim women who have been discriminated against by personal law
 Could
 jiske baad kai muslim mahilaon ne supreme court main arji daayar kii he, jinamein tripal talaak, bahu vivaah or halaala ke praavdhaan ko chunauti di he
 The Supreme Court had issued a notice to the Central Government and other parties in the matter
 shuukravaar ko lau board ne mukhya taur par yachikaaon ko khaarij karne ke liye die ye aadhaar:- yachika main jo sawaal uthaae gaye hai wo nyaayik samiksha ke daayre main nahin aate
 - Personal law cannot be challenged
 - samjik sudhaar ke naam par personal lau ko dobaaraa se nahin likhaa ja saktaa
 - Petition challenging triple divorce in Muslim society is outside the purview of the court
 - supreme court ke kai puraane faisle hai, jinamein kaha gaya he ki yachika main uthaae gaye sawaal nyaayik samiksha ke daayre ke baahar he
 - The Supreme Court has said in the 1981 Krishna Singh case that the Supreme Court cannot judge the validity of the provision of Muslim personal law for marriage, divorce and alimony
 - personal lau ko chunauti nahin di ja sakati, kyonki aisa karnaa samvidhan kaa ulanghan he
 Personal law is protected under Articles 25, 26 and 29 of the Constitution
 - muslim personal lau shaadi, talaak or guzaare-bhatte ke praavdhaan kii vyakhya karata he
 It is based on the Quran and Sharia
 is par court apni vyakhya nahin kar sakati
 - Personal law cannot be challenged because doing so would violate Part-3 of the Constitution
 - samvidhan ke anuchhed-44 main unifrm civil code kii baat kii gayi he lekin wo badhyakaari nahin he
 The hawala of the constitution has been responded to by the Personal Law Board on notice in the form of this affidavit
 board ne halafname main ye kaha he ki personal lau kaa mul strot quran he
 In such a situation, its validity cannot be tested
 muslim personal lau ko validity ke aadhaar par chunauti nahin di ja sakati
 Part 3 of the constitution does not touch personal law and in such a situation the Supreme Court cannot review personal law
 dharmik muddon par paidaa hone vaale vivaad main dharmik kitabon kaa hi sahaara liya ja saktaa he
 The provision is open to the wife
 The affidavit also states that according to the Shariah, marriage goes by mutual agreement and there should be peace for a happy marriage
 lekin miyaan-bivi ke rishton main agar khatas ho jaae or nafrat paidaa ho jaae to rahanaa mushkil ho jaataa he
 In such a situation, when there is no purpose of marriage, it is better to remain separate and it is necessary to end the marriage, so that both can start another life
 pati talaak le saktaa he or patni ke liye khulaa kaa praavdhaan he
 All jurists agree that the husband has the right to divorce
 ye adhikaar sharia detaa he kyonki pati faisla le saktaa he or use apni bhaawanaaon par zyada kaabo rahata he
 In the case of alimony for the Iddat period, the affidavit states that a Muslim is allowed four weddings, this is a social and moral requirement and is also a provision of sympathy for women
 muslim personal lau board ne kaha ki jahaan tak gujaarey-bhatte yani mentanence kaa sawaal he to muslim vooman (protection of rhite on divorce) act bana he
 Under this, there is a provision of alimony for the 'iddat' period
 saath hi bacchon kii paidaaish se lekar do saal tak mentanence kaa praavdhaan he
 If after the completion of the Iddat, the woman cannot survive and her second marriage is not possible and the magistrate is satisfied with the plea of the woman, then he can instruct the relative of the woman to do the standard life maintenance of the woman
 is tarah muslim mahilaon ke liye mentanence kaa adhikaar diya gaya he
 In this case, the petitions filed in this case should be dismissed

 is dhara ko lekar bhartiya raajnneeti main uthaa patake hoti rahati he
 Many political parties hold it responsible for separatism in Jammu and Kashmir
 vakt bevakt is dhara ko hataane kii maang uthati rahati he
 What is Article 370 Article 370 is a special Article of the Indian Constitution
 jojammu-kashmirarajya ko bharat main anya rajyon ke mukaable vishesh adhikaar yaa vishesh darza detii he
 Article 370 of Part 21 relating to temporary, transitional and special provisions in the Indian Constitution was prepared with the special intervention of Jawaharlal Nehru
 raja hari singh ne rakhaa tha prastaavdesh aaazaad hone ke baad choti-choti riyasaton ko bhartiya sangh main shaamil kiya gaya tha
 When the process of incorporating Jammu and Kashmir into the Indian Union started, Pakistan-supported tribesmen attacked there
 kashmir ke tatkaaleen raja hari singh ne hi kashmir ke bharat main vilay kaa prastaav rakhaa tha
 Article 370 was made of section 306A
 At that time there was no time to complete the constitutional process of merging Kashmir with India
 isi halaat ko dekhte hue sangheey samvidhan sabha main gopalswami ingar ne dhara 306-e kaa praaroop prastut kiya tha, jo baad main dhara 370 ban gai
 Because of which Jammu and Kashmir has got different rights from other states of India
 jammu kashmir ko mili hai kai vishesh adhikardhaara 370 ke praavdhaanon ke mutabik sansad ko jammu-kashmir ke bare main raksha, videsh maamle or sanchaar ke vishay main kanoon banane kaa adhikaar he lekin kisi anya vishay se sambandhit kaanoon ko lagu karwaane ke liye kendra ko rajya sarkaar kaa anumodan lenaa padataa he
 Due to this special record, Article 356 of the Constitution does not apply to the state of Jammu and Kashmir
 is kaaran raashtrapati ke paas rajya ke samvidhan ko barkhaast karne kaa adhikaar nahin he
 The Urban Land Law of 1976 does not apply to Jammu and Kashmir
 dhara 370 ke tahat bhartiya naagarik ko vishesh adhikaar praapt rajyon ke alaava bharat main kahin bhi bhoomi kareedne kaa adhikaar he
 That is, people of other states of India cannot buy land in Jammu and Kashmir
 bhartiya samvidhan kii dhara 360 yani desh main vittiya apatkaal lagane vaala praavdhaan jammu-kashmir par lagu nahin hota
 The merger of Jammu and Kashmir into India was a much greater necessity and to carry out this work some special rights were given to the people of Kashmir at that time under Section 370
 jo is rajya ko anya rajyon se alag banaate hai
 These are the special things of section 370
 Citizens of Jammu and Kashmir have dual citizenship
 jammu-kashmir kaa rashtradhvaj alag hota he
 The tenure of the Legislative Assembly here is 6 years, while the legislatures of other states of India have a term of 5 years
 jammu-kashmir main bharat ke rashtradhvaj yaa rashtriya pratikon kaa apmaan aparaadh nahin he
 Here the orders of the Supreme Court of India are not valid
 bharat kii sansad jammu-kashmir ke sambandh main atyant simit kshetra main kanoon bana sakati he
 If a woman from Jammu and Kashmir marries a person from any other state in India, the woman's citizenship will end
 iske vipareet yadi koi kashmiri mahila pakistan ke kisi vyakti se vivaah karti he, to use bhi jammu-kashmir kii naagarikta mil jaati he
 Due to Section 370, RTI is not applicable in Kashmir, RTE is also not applicable and CAG is also not applicable here
 yahaan mahilaon par shariat kanoon lagu he
 The panchayat has no authority in Kashmir
 kashmir main kaam karne vaale chaparasi ko aaj bhi vetan ke taur par 2500 rupaye hi milte hai
 Minority Hindus and Sikhs in Kashmir do not get 16% reservation
 dhara 370 kii vajah se kashmir main baahar ke log jameen nahin kharid sakate hai
 Due to this Article 370, Pakistanis living in Kashmir also get Indian citizenship
